< text>
My family threw me a retirement party at the Brewery for about 140 people with Peter White and the Dole Humphries band.   The staff was so organized, helpful and fun.  The taco bar was amazing and the bar staff keep every body happy and drinking.  The beer selection is huge and the flavors wonderful.  They arranged the tables like we needed, they handled every little request.  They were calm and my family had to chance to relax and enjoy the night. It was a PERFECT night.</text>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
We had the rehearsal dinner for our wedding at Wolf Creek Brewery and hosted about 100 people. The event was excellent!  We had the food catered by Wolf Creek restaurant (taco bar), and it was delicious. They even boxed up the left-overs and we enjoyed them on our mini-moon following our wedding. Everyone commented on how great the beer was, but beyond that, Wolf Creek was great about letting us setup the space, which was very conducive to a relaxed-good time. Our guests played lawn games and enjoyed the casual atmosphere, which is exactly what we wanted! Would highly recommend Wolf Creek Brewery for your event!</review>

< Review>
While some may think the location is not the best, I think it is a great place to get away to somewhere quiet! The beer is always good and the servers are helpful. The patio has improved greatly over the past couple of years, and the Corn Hole league is a plus! Beer of choice for me would be the Outlaw IPA (seasonal beer, unfortunately). I have been many times before, and plan on going many more times in the future.</Review>

<rate>5<//rate><Review>The Golden Eagle Ale is one of the best beers around.  If you see it on tap someplace give it a try.
I often pick up a 5.2 gallon directly from the tasting room for my kegerator, its that good.
The staff there is really nice but the place is hard to find. Often GPS will send you someplace south of Newhall Ranch Road when the gate to the Rye Canyon Loop is north of it off of the Kelly Johnson Parkway. The complex the brewery is in was once the old Lockheed Skunk Works site called Rye Canyon back in the 60's.

That goes a long way toward explaining why the place is so hard to find.<//Review><pictures>None< /pictures>< resp>
None< /resp>

<text>Bought a few big tools from this place over the years. In general, they are a very expensive pawn shop. They play the mark up game to the point that their used stuff is at least as expensive as new and then they put a 40-50% "discount" on it. Which means, it's a sham. Just know that going in.

I have no problem with their game IF they are negotiable on their pricing (I mean it's a pawn shop, right?!). Most times they are, but recently the posted price has become a "good deal", a sort of take-it-or-leave-it attitude. Why all these people keep saying "this is the Cambodian restuarant"? Since, all the food are Thai dishes.

@The owner, that would sound better for you to say this, "This is the Cambodian-Owner restaurant, but we are serving Thai food" that would be the correct information.

They have no coconut milk and curries paste. Some dishes like salad. And all dishes you have at Angkor Borie, probably the same menu as other Thai restaurants in Bay area. Please stop confusing us and also stop feeding us false information.

Those food you were talking about are Thai food.

I would love to try Cambodian too. But, I wont get confused between Thai food and Cambodian food.< /Review>

< Text>
I always have a great experience at Smiles For Health.  I went to one dentist my whole life prior to moving to Californian a few years ago, so I was uncertain to say the least about finding a new dentist. Dr. Zorro is kind, professional, and great at what she does. Taylor and the other staff are excellent. <UserId.>114391179533979438255< /UserId.>< review>
I have been going to Smiles for Health for about two years. The practice is very clean, and has all top-of-the-line equipment.

They are always extremely friendly and professional when contacting me about appointments, questions, etc. As soon as you walk into the office for your appointment they check you in, ask you if you need any water, etc.

< text>
You must pay at the front gate to enter if you are here for a softball tournament.
The issue is, not enough restroom facilities to accommodate the amount of people. To make it worse, the men's restroom has two urinals out of order for the past 2 months. You are not allowed to bring in any food or drinks besides water. When we attempted to purchase a hamburger,  they were out of buns. This is the 1st day of the tournament. How can you be out of the necessities? You forbid me to bring in my own food and you can't provide food on the 1st morning of a tournament? Brutal.
If you have an early morning game, parking won't be a problem. If not, good luck. Parking is horrendous.
The fields are better than average. There is no shade for the players nor the parents so be prepared.
The drive to the park from the freeway consists of about 12+ signal lights. Give yourself additional time because you will hit at least 6 of those lights and most intersections are large so you'll be waiting a bit longer than your average light.</text>

Domino's has been my family's favorite pizza over the years. We had a location in Petaluma that was closed several years ago. But now that Domino's is back in out town we are very excited. However, the quality has gone down dramatically.  The workers are not courteous. They make me wait several minutes at the counter and pretty much yell at each other to help a customer at the counter. < Review>
When driving from Phoenix to LA, this is always one of my stops.  It is convenient, always clean, and my truck gets better mileage on their gas.   They do offer both regular gas and deisel at fair rates.  The store contains everything you expect from a gas station convenience store, along with slot machines.  The outside restrooms are only open during the day.  At night you will need to use the restrooms inside the store, if needed.

Nearby you have food options such as Panda Express, Taco Bell, and Ruby Tuesday.  There is also a 24-hour Starbucks, which is a godsend on long trips.</Review>
